important! important! Let‚Äôs talk about the shortcomings:
1. I ordered some personal items for takeout and came with a box of cut fruits, but the hotel does not have a robot to deliver it. I called the front desk and reported that it would not be delivered because of food safety management issues. I had to go to the bar to get it myself. As a hotel at this price, this should not be the case. .
2. The usual drinks and snacks in the indoor bar are normally given as free gifts without price tags and consumption tips. However, when checking out, I was told that there was a charge for consumption. Although they were waived in the end without payment, it was serious. msg:After a long time, I finally have time to write a review
The overall experience is average, but the price is cheap and the service attitude is okay
advantage:
1. The biggest advantage should be the service. We stayed in three rooms for two nights. One room had a broken air conditioner on the first day. As compensation, the front desk provided two breakfast buffets for the second day.
2. Convenient transportation, the subway station is next to the hotel, which makes it easy to travel
3. The price is very cheap, only six or seven hundred

Then talk about the shortcomings
1. The room landscape is outrageous, facing a large area of unfinished buildings, the so-called construction site landscape.
2. The room is extremely small
3. The facilities are inoperable, and the rubber ***** on the toilet door falls off, causing water to leak out
4. As a hotel in such a tall building, Hilton actually chose to arrange the guest rooms on the lower floors of the building. All other hotels I have stayed in are arranged on the top floor
5. The gym is not 24 hours a day. Go to the door at 11 o'clock in the evening and put a huge sign to write that it is closed. Although you can still enter by swiping your room card, the announcement is very uncomfortable. It is recommended to change it to unsupervised at night and use it independently. Will be much better
6. The bed linen is not clean, and the feet were bitten by bugs after taking a bath and going to bed
7. Check out the consultation and check-in experience, and give true feedback. The hotel said that it is impossible for it to have a sanitary problem, and will investigate it. Is it possible that emmmm I still wronged you, and then said that the next time I come to live will be upgraded, but there is a high probability that it will not be the next time. Would choose this one
8. As a 17-year-old guest who made a reservation with his own ID, paid and paid the deposit for three rooms, it was extremely difficult to check in early due to the delay of the family‚Äôs flight, saying that it did not comply with Hilton‚Äôs internal management system, and as far as I know At the age of sixteen and have economic income, it is in line with the full capacity to check in.
